CIN .: L65190GJ1994PLC021012 COMPLEX, MUMBAI 400051, INDIA.G ICICI BANK TERMS AND CONDITIONS: FACILITY OVERDRAFT AGAINST AA- AND ABOVE RATED BONDS PROPOSED LIMIT ("LIMIT") 100.0 MILLION EXISTING LIMIT 7 50.0 MILLION SUB-LIMIT(S) INTERCHANGEABILITY PURPOSE FOR MEETING WORKING CAPITAL REQUIREMENT. SECURITY PLEDGE OF APPROVED SECURITIES IN THE NAME OF THE BORROWER SO AS TO MAINTAIN AN ASSET COVER RATIO 111.11%. THE PLEDGE OF BONDS WILL BE SUBJECT TO SECTION 19(2) AND 19(3) OF THE BANKING REGULATION ACT, 1949. MARGINS 1.11 VALIDITY OF FACILITY DECEMBER 15, 2020 INTEREST THE RATE OF INTEREST STIPULATED BY ICICI BANK SHALL BE SUM OF I-MCLR-GM AND "SPREAD" PER ANNUM, SUBJECT TO MINIMUM RATE OF I-MCLR-6M, PLUS APPLICABLE INTEREST TAX OR OTHER STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY, ON THE PRINCIPAL AMOUNT OF THE LOAN REMAINS OUTSTANDING EACH DAY. AS ON DATE THE I-MCLR-6M IS 8.15% AND SPREAD IS 1.50%. IN CASE THERE IS ANY CHANGE IN THE REGULATORY REQUIREMENTS APPLICABLE TO THE FACILITY PERTAINING TO PROVISIONING NORMS AND/OR RISK WEIGHTAGE, THEN THE BANK MAY REVISE THE SPREAD TO REFLECT THE REGULATORY CHANGE IN ORDER TO STABILIZE THE SYSTEM OF MCLR RATE CALCULATION, RBI MAY ALLOW BANKS TO CHANGE THE METHODOLOGY FOR COMPUTATION OF MCLR RATE FROM TIME TO TIME. IN CASE THERE IS CHANGE IN MCLR RATE DUE TO CHANGE IN THE METHODOLOGY FOR COMPUTATION OF MCLR RATE, THE "SPREAD" WOULD APPROPRIATELY BE RESET. INTEREST PAYMENT FREQUENCY INTEREST WOULD BE PAYABLE MONTHLY, ON THE LAST DATE OF EACH MONTH. ICI BANK MARKET CAPITAL OLKATA- 19 * REGD. MARGINS 1.11 VALIDITY OF FACILITY DECEMBER 15, 2020 INTEREST THE RATE OF INTEREST STIPULATED BY ICICI BANK SHALL BE SUM OF I-MCLR-GM AND "SPREAD" PER ANNUM, SUBJECT TO MINIMUM RATE OF I-MCLR-6M, PLUS APPLICABLE INTEREST TAX OR OTHER STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY, ON THE PRINCIPAL AMOUNT OF THE LOAN REMAINS OUTSTANDING EACH DAY. IN CASE THERE IS ANY CHANGE IN THE REGULATORY REQUIREMENTS APPLICABLE TO THE FACILITY PERTAINING TO PROVISIONING NORMS AND/OR RISK WEIGHTAGE, THEN THE BANK MAY REVISE THE SPREAD TO REFLECT THE REGULATORY CHANGE IN ORDER TO STABILIZE THE SYSTEM OF MCLR RATE CALCULATION, RBI MAY ALLOW BANKS TO CHANGE THE METHODOLOGY FOR COMPUTATION OF MCLR RATE FROM TIME TO TIME.
